# summary TLSW gives same output

    Code
      summary(x.TLSW)
    Output
      Spectral estimation was performed:

      -maximum wavelet scale analysed is scale 6.
      -boundary handling was used.
      -----------

      -maximum wavelet scale analysed is scale 6.
      -boundary handling was used.
